 2
 Then the Urine Pouch made for astronauts, after a few years a condom-like pouch for astronauts

 3
 The system of defecation was the same for the Apollo mission, the method for urination was changed to the old system for potty for the Apollo Moon mission
 lekin peshaab ke liye tarika thodaa badla gaya
 Pouches made for urination were attached to a valve

 Due to the fierce uproar over the NRC, the Rajya Sabha could not have a zero hour and a question hour and in total the proceedings could only last 12 minutes
 assam main enarasi kaa bahupratikshit doosraa or antim draft aaj jari hua he
 The first draft of the NRC, considered as evidence for the identity of the citizens of Assam, was released on the midnight of 31 December and 1 January
 aaj jari duusare or antim draft par rajyasabha main congress, sapa or tiemasi ke saansadon ne hangaamaa kiya
 As soon as Speaker m Venkaiah Naidu asked for a zero hour in the House, Trinamool Congress' Derek Obrine raised the NRC issue
 unki party ke sadasyon ke saath hi congress or sapa ke sadasyon ne bhi enarasi ke mudde parattkaal charchaa kii maanki
 On this, Naidu said that he has neither received any notice nor any letter to discuss the issue
 unhone kaha ki aaj kuch sadasyon ne unase mulaakaat kii or kaha ki aaj vah NRC kaa mudda sadan main uthaanaa chaahate hai
 The Chairman also said that he himself requested the Home Minister to come to the House so that the questions of the members could be answered

 He said that Home Minister Rajnath Singh is present in the House and he would like the Home Minister to present his stand on the NRC issue
 chaar baar kaarywahi sthagitvenkaiya naidu ne hangaamaa kar rahe sadasyon se kaha ki vah kaarywahi chalane den anyathaa sadan sthagit kar diya jayega

 In order to deal with the ever increasing hoax calls in Mumbai, the police has taken such a step, which may benefit the investigation of the common man and the poor
 police ne bina idi card dikhaae pisio se phone karne par pabandi laga di he, isliye jin logon ke paas koi pahachaanapatr nahin hoga, unke liye public phone booth se phone karnaa mumkin nahin rah jayega
 Mumbai Police Commissioner Dr Satyapal Singh said, "under the order we have given, people who want to call from pcos will not only have to show ID card, but also have to write their information in the register of PCO operator
" is tarah agar koi aadmi galat kol karata he, to police ko jaanch ke dauraan phayda mil sakegaa
 According to Dr
 Singh, this is an anti-terror step
 unhone kaha, jis tarah mumbai police real estate waalon se kiraayedaaron kii jaankaree maangati he, mobile phone ke simcard bechney waalon se card kharidne waalon kii jaankaree maangati he, usee tarah ab pisio chaalkon se bhi phone karne waalon kii jaankaree maangi jaaegi
 Actually, the number of hoax callers in Mumbai is constantly increasing, and usually such calls come to inform about the placing of bombs etc
 in a mall or railway station
 aise kol pisio booth se bhi kiye jate hai, jisase collar ko dhundhna naammumkin ho jaataa he
 Experts say that the government has to spend millions of rupees to stop such false calls made by spending one rupee
 jab bhi aise hoks kol aate hai, police kii taraf se sabase pehle bomb dyspozal squad ko bheja jaataa he, jisamen bam niskriy karne vaale ek adhikari ke saath kam se kam 10 pulicekarmi hote hai, or do snifer dogs bhi bheje jate hai
 Apart from these, ambulances and fire brigade trains are also called to the scene for any kind of emergency
 iske baad kisi bhi mal ko puri tarah khaali karakar bam dhundne main kam se kam chaar ghante tak kharch ho jate hai
 In such a situation, if the bomb is reported in a train, then there is loss of lakhs of rupees for the railway as well as for the passengers
 tippaniyan It is not that the investigating agencies are not doing anything to stop such calls
 arpeef, yani railway protection force ne to hoks kol kar pareshaan karne waalon ke khilaaf aatankwaad virdohi kanoon ke tahat karrwai karne kaa man bana liya tha
 According to the police, so far, under the sections of IPC, action on hoax callers can be given only six months
 aamtaur par adaalatein bhi aise shararti logon ke khilaaf sakht rukh nahin apana paatin, kyonki zyaadaatar maamalon main collar kaa makasad majaak hota he
 Now it has to be seen that how effective this action of Mumbai Police Commissioner proves, because in today's era where every other person has the facility of mobile phone, from the pcos, in fact, such poor people call, for whom ID always It is not possible to keep a card
 mumbai police ke kamishnar dow satyapal singh ne kaha, hamane jo aadesh diya he, uske tahat pisio se phone karne ke icchhuk logon ko na sirf idi card dikhaanaa hoga, balki pisio chalaane vaale ke register main apni jaankaree bhi likhavani hogi
 In this way, if a man makes a wrong call, the police will get the benefit during the investigation
 dow singh ke mutabik yah anti-teror step he
 He said, just as Mumbai Police asks for information of tenants from real estate people, mobile phone SIM card vendors demand information about those who buy cards, similarly PCO drivers will also ask for information about callers
 darasal, mumbai main hoks cholero kii sankhya lagaataar badhati ja rahi he, or aamtaur par aise kol kisi mal yaa railway stesan main bam aadi rakhaa hone kii jaankaree dene ke liye aate hai
 Such calls are also made from the PCO booth, which makes it impossible to locate the caller
 jaankaron kaa kahana he ki ek rupaya kharch kar kiye gaye aise jhuthe kol ko rokane ke liye sarkaar ko lakhon rupee kharch karne padate hai
 Whenever such hoax calls are received, the police are first sent to the Bomb Disposal Squad, which consists of at least 10 policemen, along with one bomb neutralizing officer, and two sniffer dogs
 inke alaava kisi bhi tarah kii emergency ke liye ambulance or fire brigade kii gadiyon ko bhi ghatnasthal par bulaayaa jaataa he

e
, the Railway Protection Force, had decided to take action against the harassers under the anti-terrorism law by making hoax calls

 Huh
